2&quot;\n  where (O.status in { 'final', 'amended' }\n  and O.code in &quot;HIVtesttypeCodes&quot; \n  and O.value in &quot;Reactive&quot;\n  and &quot;Age_greater_than_18_months&quot;)\n\n  /* Output
